<script>
function appealHide(){
    ["appeal-status","appeal-form","appeal-success"].forEach(id=>{
        document.getElementById(id).style.display="none";
    });
}
function appealStatus(){
    appealHide();
    document.getElementById("appeal-status").style.display="block";
}
function appealForm(){
    appealHide();
    document.getElementById("appeal-form").style.display="block";
}
function appealSubmit(){
    appealHide();
    document.getElementById("appeal-success").style.display="block";
}
</script>

<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_54fee5-15"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Step 3:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Then, click on the &#8220;</span><b>Check Status</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">&#8221; button.</span></span></li>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_de3349-50 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_3112ec-ef"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Sassa Status Check Online Through Official Website?</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>You can check your status online at srd.sassa.gov.za by following these steps</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_04de92-e7 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_5a91d4-65"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Step 1:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Visit the </span><b>&#8220;Official Website of SASSA</b>&#8220;<span style="font-weight: 400;">:</span><a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">  <span style="font-weight: 400;">https://srd.sassa.gov.za/</span></a></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_b2750e-16"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Step 2:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Click on the &#8220;</span><b>Click here to Proceed</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">&#8221; button</span>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_02e7b6-08"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Step 3:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> After Click this &#8220;<strong>Button</strong>&#8221; move to the next page.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_19dd83-4f"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Step 4:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Show this page and enter your &#8220;<strong>Details</strong>&#8220;</span>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_933a27-5d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Step 5: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">Click on the &#8220;</span><b>South African ID of Applicant</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">&#8221; box shown below the image</span>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_9ca297-12"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Step 6:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Click on the &#8220;</span><b>Phone Number Used to Submit Your Application</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">&#8221; box shown below the image.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_d5cb7f-e9"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Step 7:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Then, Click on the &#8220;</span><b>Submit</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">&#8221; button</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_97e4d9-9a"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Step 8:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Finally show your </span><b>&#8220;SASSA Current Status&#8221;</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">.&nbsp;</span></span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>



<blockquote class="wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">We hope all confusion is clear about SASSA Status Check. If you have any problem checking your status please comment your issue in the comment box.</span></p>
</blockquote>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_c9d1ce-3f alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_39021f-b9"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>SASSA Status Check By Moya App</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Another method I like is checking the SRD application status through the Moya App. You only need an internet connection to download the app; it is a data-free method.</span></p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large is-resized"><img decoding="async" width="1024" height="1024" src="https://sassa-status-check.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Status-Check-By-Moya-App-1024x1024.png" alt="SASSA Status Check By Moya App" class="wp-image-6092" style="width:412px;height:auto" srcset="https://sassa-status-check.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Status-Check-By-Moya-App-1024x1024.png 1024w, https://sassa-status-check.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Status-Check-By-Moya-App-300x300.png 300w, https://sassa-status-check.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Status-Check-By-Moya-App-150x150.png 150w, https://sassa-status-check.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Status-Check-By-Moya-App-768x768.png 768w, https://sassa-status-check.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Status-Check-By-Moya-App.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></figure>
</div>


<p>The Moya app can be downloaded without the internet and you can check your status without it. You need to follow these steps:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_e5fe21-e2 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_738bbd-1e"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_logOut kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M9 21H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h4"/><polyline points="16 17 21 12 16 7"/><line x1="21" y1="12" x2="9" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Install the &#8220;<strong>Moya App&#8221;</strong> from the <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=nu.bi.moya&amp;hl=en&amp;gl=US" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><strong>PlayStore</strong></a> (This step requires an internet connection).</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_dc1bb1-2c"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_logOut kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M9 21H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h4"/><polyline points="16 17 21 12 16 7"/><line x1="21" y1="12" x2="9" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">You can open the app after downloading it, navigate to the &#8220;<strong>Discovery</strong>&#8221; tab, and select &#8220;<strong>SASSA Grant</strong>&#8220;.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_75d2a0-db"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_logOut kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M9 21H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h4"/><polyline points="16 17 21 12 16 7"/><line x1="21" y1="12" x2="9" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Select &#8220;<strong>SASSA SRD Status</strong>&#8221; from the menu and click on &#8220;<strong>Application Status</strong>&#8220;.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_bc3ecd-16"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_logOut kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M9 21H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h4"/><polyline points="16 17 21 12 16 7"/><line x1="21" y1="12" x2="9" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Enter your &#8220;<strong>ID Number&#8221;</strong> and <strong>&#8220;Mobile Number&#8221;</strong> and click &#8220;<strong>Submit</strong>&#8220;.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_3a4d70-aa"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_logOut kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M9 21H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h4"/><polyline points="16 17 21 12 16 7"/><line x1="21" y1="12" x2="9" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Your <strong>&#8220;Status Will Be Displayed</strong>&#8221; promptly after you click the &#8220;<strong>Submit</strong>&#8221; button.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_4f13ac-8b alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_bb3f6b-21"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>SASSA Status Check Through SMS</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>You can also check your SASSA grant status through SMS&nbsp;by following these steps:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_fed724-50 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_cd100b-36"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Your mobile <strong>&#8220;Device Text Messaging App&#8221;</strong> should be open.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_caf15f-c4"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Please type the message &#8220;<strong>SASSA ID Number</strong>&#8220;. Your &#8220;<strong>South African ID Number&#8221; </strong>should be valid.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_701bef-bd"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Please send this message to &#8220;<strong>082 046 8553&#8243;</strong>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_a66134-f0"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">You will receive a response with information regarding your &#8220;<strong>SASSA R350 Grant Status</strong>&#8220;.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_b4f774-a2 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_7cff16-d2"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>SASSA Status Check Through Whats App</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>You can also check the status of your application via WhatsApp if you are unable to access the portal. Follow these steps:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_9a5618-4e kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_0d2b1b-60"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_logIn kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15 3h4a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2h-4"/><polyline points="10 17 15 12 10 7"/><line x1="15" y1="12" x2="3" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">The first step is to add the number &#8220;<strong>082 046 8553&#8243;</strong> to your WhatsApp contacts.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_608c73-cd"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_logIn kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15 3h4a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2h-4"/><polyline points="10 17 15 12 10 7"/><line x1="15" y1="12" x2="3" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Send the word &#8220;<strong>SASSA</strong>&#8221; to that &#8220;<strong>WhatsApp Number</strong>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_52a981-f0"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_logIn kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15 3h4a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2h-4"/><polyline points="10 17 15 12 10 7"/><line x1="15" y1="12" x2="3" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">If you receive a response, reply with the word &#8220;<strong>STATUS</strong>&#8220;</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_ded14f-39"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_logIn kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15 3h4a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2h-4"/><polyline points="10 17 15 12 10 7"/><line x1="15" y1="12" x2="3" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">When asked for a<strong> &#8220;Reference Number</strong>&#8221; in the chat, reply with &#8220;<strong>YES</strong>&#8221; (Only reply with &#8220;<strong>YES</strong>&#8221; if you already have the reference number).</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_ba5871-58"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_logIn kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15 3h4a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2h-4"/><polyline points="10 17 15 12 10 7"/><line x1="15" y1="12" x2="3" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">When you are asked for your &#8220;<strong>Mobile Number&#8221;</strong>, provide it (the number you used during SRD grant registration).</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_705cfb-07"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_logIn kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15 3h4a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2h-4"/><polyline points="10 17 15 12 10 7"/><line x1="15" y1="12" x2="3" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Reply with your<strong> &#8220;Reference Number</strong> in the chat after that.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_0b44ff-75"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_logIn kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15 3h4a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2h-4"/><polyline points="10 17 15 12 10 7"/><line x1="15" y1="12" x2="3" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">You will receive a <strong>&#8220;Response Detailing Your Current Status&#8221;.</strong></span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_c34b2c-f3 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_8c91bc-28"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>SASSA Status Check By Call</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>The SASSA <strong>call center number 0800 601 011</strong> is available for anyone who wishes to verify their application or payment status on the phone rather than through the SASSA website or message system.</p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_bec0ad-f0 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>SASSA Status Check Online &#8211; Video Guide</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>

<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box5674_64abf9-b2"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-image-inner-intrisic-container"><div class="kadence-info-box-image-intrisic kt-info-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-image-inner-intrisic"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" src="https://sassa-status-check.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2022/07/cropped-Sassa-Status-Check-e1659039310836-1.jpg" alt="Sassa Status Check" width="248" height="240" class="kt-info-box-image wp-image-6050"/></div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><h2 class="kt-blocks-info-box-title"><strong>What Is SASSA?</strong></h2><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text">The South African Social Security Agency is known as SASSA. Sassa administers social grants to people who are “vulnerable to poverty and in need of state support” as a means of improving their standard of living.<br><br>Everything you need to know about the SASSA status check for the SRD grant, including the payments dates when it can be collected. The R350 Social Relief Grant Payment schedule is announced each month by the South African Social Security Agency – SASSA.<br><br>This is the organization that has been put in charge of distributing and providing government assistance for the special Covid-19 Social Relief benefit. They are also responsible for disability grant recipients and child support grant beneficiaries.<br><br>A monthly financial aid program is provided to such individuals in order to support them. Beneficiaries must however meet official eligibility criteria in order to qualify for such grants.</p></div></div></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_49fcef-b2 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_8b2875-4d"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Who Can Use SASSA </b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>SASSA, managed by the Department of Social Development in South Africa, provides monthly grants to individuals falling into the following categories: Older persons (aged 60 and above), persons with disabilities, and war veterans.</p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_09e803-1a alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_c25cc1-0b"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Eligibility and Criteria for SASSA Grant</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>If you want to apply for an SRD R350 grant in 2026, you must meet the following criteria:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_9d1754-c5 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_7f0dec-61"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">You must be a South African citizen, a recognized refugee, or an asylum seeker with valid documentation.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_5f3308-05"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">The applicant must reside in South Africa.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_e70b3b-de"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">The age must be between 18 and 60.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_f17681-23"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Earnings should not exceed R624 per month.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_204490-fa"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">You cannot receive any other government social grant.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_0741b7-e6"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">There must be insufficient resources to cover basic needs.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_e3adec-b0"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">The applicant must be unemployed and have no other source of income.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_81feda-4b"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">The assets or investments required to survive are insufficient.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_68a5ac-e9"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Cannot contribute to UIF or receive benefits from it.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_d553ce-16"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">NSFAS stipends must not be received.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_4d349b-30"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">A person should not refuse to accept an employment or educational opportunity based on unreasonable grounds.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_21cb8f-64"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Applicants must not reside in state-funded housing.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_d01af7-a0"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_chevronsRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="13 17 18 12 13 7"/><polyline points="6 17 11 12 6 7"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">A clean criminal record is required.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_93c5e3-84 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_65acc6-0b"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>How to Apply for SASSA SRD Grant?</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>SRD grants can be applied for via WhatsApp, SASSA&#8217;s chatbot, or the SASSA website. As this is the simplest way to apply, I will explain how to do so via the website:</p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_1386cc-75 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_38f864-26"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Access the SASSA Official Website</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_a9b934-46 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_f55681-86"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Visit the SASSA official website at <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/said" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://srd.sassa.gov.za/said</a>. The &#8220;How do I apply for this SRD Grant&#8221; section can be accessed by clicking the &#8220;click here to apply online&#8221; button.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_898998-0f alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_10104b-1d"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Provide Your Phone Number</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_8e92ea-08 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_bbfe37-2d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Lastly, enter the phone number registered to your name. Make sure it is active and accessible to you at all times.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_699066-12 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_794347-9f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Verify OTP (One Time Pin)</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_6595b6-49 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_7c6a80-27"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">You will receive the OTP code on your cell phone. Click &#8220;Verify OTP&#8221; after entering the code on the website.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_7304ac-f9 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_8941f0-98"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Agree to the Terms &amp; Conditions</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_7c6651-c3 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_719cec-95"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">The terms and conditions will now be presented for your review and agreement. To proceed to the next step, you must agree with them.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_d6db07-ba alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_f4c1c7-56"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Fill Out Personal Information</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_1f6e22-f3 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_1cf3a5-e2"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Please provide your ID number, name, surname, gender, date of birth, email address, residential address, contact information, citizenship status, employment status, and financial information.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_b318f2-54 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_36624e-14"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Add Banking Details</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_4f63a6-38 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_692e86-7f"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">A bank account is required to receive grants. The next step is to provide your bank account information.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_1c73eb-59 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_09ebc8-f4"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Upload the Required Documents</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_9288fc-0f kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_b40a36-cb"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">At this step, you will need to upload a copy of your original ID card or passport. Supporting documents that demonstrate your financial status and eligibility can also be submitted.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_7d57ba-8d alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_f9f79c-06"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Submit the Application</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_87da39-6b kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_0f4ea4-7d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">When you finish providing all the information, make sure you proofread it carefully to ensure everything is accurate. Proceed to submit your online application if everything is correct.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_50782c-a7 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_7e221e-4e"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Check Your SASSA Status Regularly</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_6958c8-d3 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_8199a7-42"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">If you have submitted an application, it is important to check its status regularly to stay on top of its progress and approval.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>



<blockquote class="wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-47366ebe7da9b5bedf0248918d28eaa5" style="color:#670707"><strong>Note</strong></p>



<p>Please submit your application via one channel only to avoid delays. A multiple application will not speed up the application process, but instead cause delays due to spamming.</p>
</blockquote>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_032801-f6 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_805125-88"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Speed Up Access to SRD Funds</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>If you check your SASSA SRD grant application regularly online, you can get your payment faster. The SASSA website, Moya app, WhatsApp, or call center are alternatives to waiting in long lines at SASSA offices. It is easier to access urgent social assistance with these digital options since they provide updates around the clock.</p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_669d31-9d alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_760f87-55"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Why Regularly Checking Your SASSA Status Matters?</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>The importance of keeping track of your SASSA status is due to the following reasons:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_c68d7d-9e kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_3f1b72-ed"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">It keeps you informed about the progress of your social grant application.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_910014-94"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">SASSA requirements and whether your documents are correct can be verified.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_e8480b-4a"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Keep track of payments due and access details about how grants are distributed with this tool.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_9a41c6-dd"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">We&#8217;ll let you know if there are any delays in processing your application or if a reconsideration is needed.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_630cc0-e2"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Payments and bank information can be managed more easily.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_746e9e-96"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">We will address any issues you may have with your social assistance as soon as possible.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_afb96e-8c"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Ensures that you receive your benefits and financial support in a timely manner.</span></li>
</ul></div>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_1bca76-cc alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_6c971b-dd"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>SASSA Status Check Online for SRD Payment Dates 2026</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p>The South African government announced that there is no specific date for receiving SRD grants, and the payment schedule will be shared every month at the end of the previous month. Financial assistance will be provided to grant beneficiaries each month they qualify. The monthly status check for your payment must be performed.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="637" height="901" src="https://sassa-status-check.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Payment-Dates-for-2024-2025.jpg" alt="SASSA Payment Dates for 2024 2025" class="wp-image-6113" style="width:483px;height:auto" srcset="https://sassa-status-check.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Payment-Dates-for-2024-2025.jpg 637w, https://sassa-status-check.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Payment-Dates-for-2024-2025-212x300.jpg 212w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 637px) 100vw, 637px" /></figure>
</div>


<p></p>



<p>The payment dates for SASSA for the year 2026 are below; however, they may be delayed by public holidays or unforeseen circumstances.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-fixed-layout"><thead><tr><th>SASSA Grants</th><th>January 2026 Payment Dates</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><strong>SASSA R370 Grant / SRD R350</strong></td><td><strong>Starts from Monday 27 January 2026</strong> <strong>to Friday 31 January 2026</strong></td></tr><tr><td><strong>Old Age Grant (older person pension)</strong></td><td><strong>Friday, January 3, 2026</strong></td></tr><tr><td><strong>War Veterans Grant</strong></td><td><strong>Friday, January 3, 2026</strong></td></tr><tr><td><strong>Disability Grant</strong></td><td><strong>Monday, January 6, 2026</strong></td></tr><tr><td><strong>Care Dependency Grant</strong></td><td><strong>Monday, January 6, 2026</strong></td></tr><tr><td><strong>Child Support Grant</strong></td><td><strong>Tuesday, January 7, 2026</strong></td></tr><tr><td><strong>Foster Child Grant</strong></td><td><strong>Tuesday, January 7, 2026</strong></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>



<blockquote class="wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-adb104e1baabe3923fbb1cea11d02208" style="color:#730c0c"><strong>NOTE</strong></p>



<p>The SRD R350 grant does not have a fixed payment date. Your payment dates will be notified to you via text message each month, or you can check them via the status check every month.</p>
</blockquote>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_878c17-f1 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_7052fc-97"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Important Information About SASSA Status Check</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>Please submit all required documents electronically, there is no need to submit physical documents. Your mobile number should be active to receive updates regarding your application. Here you can easily check the status of your application.</p>



<p>Should your application be declined, you have the option of appealing monthly through the Department of Social Development. When a declined decision is not appealed, the original decision will stand.</p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_aec9e4-46 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_cb219f-de"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Keep Your Grant Application Updated</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>SRD R350 grant applicants or reapplicants since April 2022 are automatically considered until March 2026. Update your screening questionnaire responses whenever necessary to ensure the accuracy of your information.</p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_85c0c5-73 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_e0b2f6-4c"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>How to Appeal Your SASSA SRD Grant?</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>Starting from April 2022, you may appeal any rejection of your application by visiting the DSD (Department of Social Development) appeals website. Appeals are handled by ITSAA (Independent Tribunal for Social Assistance Appeals) and must be filed within 90 days of rejection:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_d416d8-ad kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_a989bc-cf"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Go to the DSD website via the link <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/appeals" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://srd.sassa.gov.za/appeals</a>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_d937b9-56"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">To lodge an appeal or check the appeal status, click the button “click here ”.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_fd7e11-ab"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">You will need to enter your 13-digit African ID card number and your registered phone number in order to request a PIN.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_e0ed00-46"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">You will receive a PIN via SMS. You will need to enter this PIN on the website.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_e8a0d7-a0"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Choose the month of your rejected grant. For each rejected SRD grant month, file a separate appeal.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_fbff45-5e"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Provide all necessary documents (e.g., last six months&#8217; bank statements, proof of residence, ID).</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_ca377a-8d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Give a concise explanation of why you are appealing.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_2f9ae5-e6"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">After attaching the documents and explaining why you are appealing, submit the form.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<blockquote class="wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p>After you submit your appeal, the independent tribunal will review it and render a decision within 60 to 90 days. If ITSAA accepts your appeal, you will receive the SRD grant payments, otherwise, you will be notified if your appeal is denied.</p>
</blockquote>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_65ac46-be alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_c53a9e-bb"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><strong>SASSA Reconsideration Status Check</strong></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>Reconsideration for May 2020 to March 2022 has ended, and no additional applications will be considered. If you would like to check the status of your reconsideration appeal, please follow the steps below:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_7b2d16-f3 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_28d436-e6"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Go to the reconsideration status check page at <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/appeals" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/reconsideration</a>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_8f7484-92"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Please enter your South African ID number and your reconsideration application phone number.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_8d386b-8c"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Send your OTP by clicking &#8220;send pin&#8221; and waiting for it to arrive on your registered phone number.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_003d79-dc"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Please enter the OTP code on the website.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_974341-f6"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">The status of your reconsideration will be displayed on the screen.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_822cc5-0f alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_8c7bda-82"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Updated Contact Details for the SASSA R350 Grant</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>You can update your contact details for the R350 grant by following these steps:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_5051cb-0d kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_5e9019-ad"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Go to the SASSA website: <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/appeals" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/contact</a>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_9a2617-1b"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Please enter your South African ID number and application ID.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_eb6910-d1"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Please double-check your information before submitting it.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_e06567-f4"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Verify your email address and provide your new phone number now.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_2577c3-88"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Select a reason for changing your phone number.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_1e8967-dc"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Please check your new phone number for an OTP. You can verify the OTP by providing it on the website.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<blockquote class="wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p>Once updated, you’ll receive notifications on your new phone for future SRD grant updates.</p>
</blockquote>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_ef0a62-be alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_f6d9a8-f9"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><strong>How To Get Sassa Grant Sent To Your Bank Account?</strong></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>Receiving payments via your bank account is probably the most convenient payment method and fastest way to receive the grant, it also means you can avoid queuing in person at the Post Office.</p>



<p>The amounts for each month will be paid into the bank account of the beneficiary as per the grant application. Please note that the bank details or cellular phone number provided for payment MUST be registered in the name of the approved applicant used in the COVID-19 R350 grant application process to make sure that payment goes to the correct recipients.</p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_5a93d8-52 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_4d87bf-db"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>How to Change SRD R350 Grant Banking Details?</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>The SASSA SRD R350 banking details can only be changed by permanent SASSA grant recipients. There is a slightly different process for South African citizens and Asylum Seekers/Special Permit holders.</p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_bb3cf3-ef alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_547789-85"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Process for South African ID Card Holders</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>If you are a holder of a South African ID Card, you must follow the following steps:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_cbe5ba-99 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_008424-9e"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Go to the SASSA official website: <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://srd.sassa.gov.za/</a>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_9b73c5-3f"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Click the &#8220;click here to proceed&#8221; button in the &#8220;South African ID Holders&#8221; section at the bottom of the page.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_f718e2-52"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Go to the &#8220;Change my banking details&#8221; tab and enter your ID Card number.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_bd3695-f6"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">SMS will be sent to your registered mobile number with a secure link.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_9f9a48-06"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Please click the link below to submit your banking information.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_1199a4-a4"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Wait for SASSA to approve your banking information after submitting the form.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_e84cb7-d5 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_c27827-dc"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Process for Asylum Seekers and Special Permit Holders</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>Follow these steps if you are an Asylum Seeker with a valid File Number or Special Permit Holder from Zimbabwe, Angola, or Lesotho:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_22161c-68 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
