<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_1e8ae8-4c"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Go to the SASSA official website: <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://srd.sassa.gov.za/</a></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_9688df-b4"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">On the &#8220;Asylum Seekers and Special Permit Holders&#8221; page, scroll to the bottom and click the &#8220;click here to proceed&#8221; button.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_fbfcc0-8f"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">The new page will open. Go to the &#8220;Lookup Payment ID&#8221; tab to collect payment at Pick &#8216;n Pay.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_e19b65-61"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">The SASSA application number, passport number, and mobile phone number need to be entered.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_a06cee-59"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">If your information is correct and valid, you will receive further instructions for updating your banking details.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_a31b9f-6d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Please wait until SASSA approves your banking details.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<blockquote class="wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p>SASSA will take up to 7 business days to approve your banking information. The next time your payment cycle is processed, you&#8217;ll receive your grant payment in your bank account.</p>
</blockquote>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_5b191a-a4 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_a006a2-3f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Important Note</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_c4b953-a0 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_567cdb-00"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">The SASSA cannot deposit grants into another&#8217;s bank account.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_864df5-d7"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">You must have a bank account and a mobile phone number in your name.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_255104-be"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Your grant payment will be deposited into your new bank account once your new bank details are verified.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_e69024-5c alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_3bc3e0-0d"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>How Do I Cancel My COVID-19 Social Relief of Distress Grant Application?</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>If your financial situation improves enough for you to no longer need COVID-19 Social Relief of Distress Grants, you may cancel them. The following steps should be followed:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_9ec374-ec kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_f62de2-56"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkSquare kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="9 11 12 14 22 4"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Go to the official SASSA portal at <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/cancellation" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/cancellation</a>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_013abf-db"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkSquare kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="9 11 12 14 22 4"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">The 13-digit ID and cellphone number you used to apply should be entered.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_bed30b-22"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkSquare kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="9 11 12 14 22 4"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Select “Send Pin” to receive an OTP.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_dd088b-be"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkSquare kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="9 11 12 14 22 4"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">To verify your identity, enter the OTP.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_707e99-f6"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkSquare kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="9 11 12 14 22 4"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Please click the &#8220;Cancel My Grant&#8221; button and confirm your cancellation.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_b09835-4e"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkSquare kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="9 11 12 14 22 4"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">SMS confirmation will be sent to your SASSA registered phone number.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<blockquote class="wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p>SASSA grants can be considered fraud and may result in criminal charges, fines, and even the ineligibility of receiving future government grants.</p>
</blockquote>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_12d811-91 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_d2289c-f4"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>How to Reinstate Your Cancelled SASSA Grant?</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>Your SRD grant can be reinstated if you previously canceled it due to improved financial circumstances, but you are now facing financial difficulties again:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_90850d-e6 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_5583a5-f4"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkSquare kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="9 11 12 14 22 4"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Go to the SASSA Web Portal at <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/reinstate" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/reinstate</a>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_a7f6c7-40"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkSquare kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="9 11 12 14 22 4"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Please enter your South African ID number and SASSA&#8217;s registered phone number.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_122b57-28"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkSquare kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="9 11 12 14 22 4"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Then click on &#8220;Send pin&#8221; and verify the OTP.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p>The following reasons can be used to reinstate a grant:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_872565-a3 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_8e7d80-f8"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Canceled in error</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_062f30-f4"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">No longer have income</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_4d2811-98"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Other</span></li>
</ul></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_3f8db0-72 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_9eac8c-4d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkSquare kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><polyline points="9 11 12 14 22 4"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Please confirm your reinstatement request.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<blockquote class="wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p>SASSA may take up to 14 days to review your reinstatement request. You will receive a notification once it has been reviewed and approved.</p>
</blockquote>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_94992e-40 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_ec3398-4f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Collecting SASSA SRD Payments for April </b></b>2026</h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>SASSA releases its payment schedules each month at the end of the previous month. The April 2026 payment dates are now available. You can only collect your SRD grant payment after the status check and after receiving an SMS notification confirming your payment each month.</p>



<p>There are three ways to collect your money:</p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_16e3a4-16 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_97d1bd-6e"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Collect via Your Bank Account</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>In the case that you selected a bank account as a payment method and provided your bank details with your SASSA application, the grant money will be deposited directly into your bank account. The money can be withdrawn from any ATM or from the bank branch.</p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_b94311-ce alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_95a437-8a"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Collect Via SASSA Card</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>SASSA Cards can be used at ATMs or SASSA-selected stores that offer free withdrawals.</p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_be27a9-5f alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_e96c2b-8c"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Using a Cash Payment Method</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>You will have to collect your grant money in cash from the local Post Office branches (SAPOs/Post Banks) or SASSA-partnered retail outlets if you did not provide bank information.</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_ac21fb-39 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_cfd984-47"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Pick n Pay</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_ed47f2-3f"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Shoprite</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_d2956d-7e"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Boxer</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_1a33da-0b"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Checkers</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_6bb574-bc"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Usave</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_39e699-98"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Spar</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>



<p>The following steps should be followed to withdraw money from SASSA-selected stores:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_971add-d2 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_2a2428-bc"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">If you want to avoid long lines, come to the SASSA-partnered store early in the morning with your South African ID card and application ID.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_1e5a21-4a"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Withdraw your grant amount from the cashier.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_e90c72-09"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">You will need to provide your ID card and application ID to the cashier.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_8379ab-68"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">They will verify your details and hand over the payment along with a receipt.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<blockquote class="wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p><wt-ignore uuid="4ff365e3-0142-43c3-90e0-45f09e4c67d1" source="wt-feature-result" data-pm-slice="0 0 []">The receipt should be kept in a safe place for future reference.</wt-ignore></p>
</blockquote>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_8c7d63-3c alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_b4e4fe-b5"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><strong>Reset Your SASSA Password</strong></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>In case you forget your SASSA password, you can reset it online easily. Follow these simple steps:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_9e3c37-45 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_f0eff7-70"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Visit the Website:</strong> Go to <a href="https://sassa.gov.za/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://sassa.gov.za</a>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_1adf09-f6"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Choose Reset Password:</strong> Select &#8220;Reset Password&#8221;.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_4cfe77-8d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Enter Your ID Number:</strong> Enter your 13-digit South African ID number.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_7ad33a-71"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Verify with OTP:</strong> Confirm your identity with the one-time password (OTP) sent to your registered cellphone.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_38573e-b5"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Set a New Password:</strong> Choose a strong password and confirm it.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_5fa96d-39"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Log In:</strong> You can now access your account using your new password.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_efb75b-19 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_d8ba65-73 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_49adec-0f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Operating Hours of SASSA Branches</b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>SASSA branches are open Monday through Friday between 7:30 AM and 8:00 AM and closed from 4:30 PM to 5:00 PM. It is important to note that opening and closing times may vary from branch to branch. Please note that SASSA branches are closed on weekends and public holidays.</p>



<p>SASSA branches recommend arriving early to avoid long wait times. While you are waiting, consider bringing essential items to keep you comfortable.</p>



<p>You can designate a family member or friend to make an application on your behalf if you cannot visit a branch due to illness or disability.</p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_7ab3fe-9f alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_f1531a-b0"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><b><strong>The Social Relief of Distress Grant</strong></b></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">A Social Relief of Distress Grant (SRD Grant) is administered in accordance with Appendix 32 of the Social Assistance Act, 2004 (Act No. 13 of 2004), and is implemented with the concurrence of the Finance Minister.</span></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The Social Relief of Distress Grant (SRD Grant) is intended for South African Citizens, Refugees, Asylum Seekers and Special Permit Holders who are between the ages of 18 and 60 years old, who have insufficient means, do not receive social grants on behalf of themselves/him, do not contribute to or qualify for UIF payments, and do not receive any other financial assistance.</span></p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_d4e880-a4 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_79f178-91"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b>Applications will be considered by SASSA only if applicants or their proxy provide the below information</b></h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_0d78b6-c0 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_7541de-a1"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">They have read and accepted the clauses in the Declaration and Consent Documents</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_c61978-b6"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Personal Details</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_5bb26b-e7"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Mobile Number (cell phone number)</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_ba6c11-70"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Lifestyle Sustainability Information and Employment Information</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_fa992d-13"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Banking Information</span></span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_ba1c02-a7 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_720274-09"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><b><strong><b>Results Of Social Relief Of Distress Grant Of R350 Application Status</b></strong></b></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The above-mentioned ways allow you to&nbsp; Check Sassa Srd R350 Status at any time . This will result in the following output, which has the following meaning, as described below.</span></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_9774fb-ff alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_8a9b79-1e"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Application Complete&nbsp;</b></b></h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Your</span><a href="https://sassa-status-check.co.za/"> <span style="font-weight: 400;">SRD Sassa</span></a> <span style="font-weight: 400;">grant will be awarded to you every month after your application has been verified after reapplication.</span></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_65c056-00 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_37150f-fe"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Bank Details Pending </b></b></h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">&nbsp;Sassa has approved your application, but you have not provided or selected a payment gateway to receive the Sassa grant. There are several payment gateways, such as cash send, bank transfer, and others. Visit srd.sassa.gov.za for information about submitting banking details.</span></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_e5db60-d5 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_9474b0-b1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Reapplication Pending</b></b></h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">As a result of the COVID-19 disaster, Sassa continues to offer the Sassa R350 grant to their unemployed citizens. However, they are required to reapply for the grant every year in order to receive the grant. If your reapplication is pending, it means that you have not submitted a new application or a new application has not been received.</span></p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_59d5d0-b4 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_f5caa6-98"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Period (e.g. November ) Pending</b></b></h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The Sassa official has received the applicant&#8217;s reapplication, but the verification process has not yet been completed. Applicants can check back in later in the month to check the latest status.</span></p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_dcebca-1f alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_4b2551-e4"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Period (e.g.November ) Approved</b></b></h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The grant application for your application has been approved, but only for the period specified. In order to confirm when the grant money will be paid, the client can check the pay date field. Sassa has not yet processed any payment for you if there was no pay date listed there.</span></p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_39bddc-8d alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_4b3f97-bf"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b>Period (e.g. November ) Declined</b></b></h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Sassa grants for the mentioned period have been declined. You were also informed of the specific reason why your Sassa application was declined by a Sassa official. As per Sassa, applicants whose grant applications have been declined can appeal or request reconsideration within 30 days of receiving the denial notice.</span></p>



<p></p>



<p><b><i>&nbsp;Some of the reasons why the application will be declined include:</i></b></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_1b9647-9e kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_2f8191-a6"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Alternative Income Source Identified</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_09832e-c4"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Uif Registered</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_b7f87f-b8"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Nsfas Registered</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_7af466-47"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Debtor</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_44fd81-57"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Referred</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_459a80-8d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Identity Verification Failed Etc</span></span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Except for the debtor, all other applicants can appeal the declined reason.</span></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_22ae72-92 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_0473d5-c7"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><b><strong>Status Canceled</strong></b></b></b></h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">It simply means that the grant has been canceled. Sassa&#8217;s website allows applicants to</span> <span style="font-weight: 400;">reinstate grants.</span></p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_0a5a59-41 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_dcc859-2a"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><b><strong><b><b>What is SASSA SRD Grant?</b></b></strong></b></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Everything you need to know about the SASSA status check for the SRD grant, including the payment dates when it can be collected. The R350 Social Relief Grant Payment schedule is announced each month by the South African Social Security Agency – SASSA. This is the organization that has been put in charge of distributing and providing government assistance for the special Covid-19 Social Relief benefit. They are also responsible for disability grant recipients and child support grant beneficiaries.</span></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">A monthly financial aid program is provided to such individuals in order to support them. Beneficiaries must however meet official eligibility criteria in order to qualify for such grants.</span></p>



<p><b>Here is the list of Grants provided by the government under the SASSA scheme.</b></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_e99d8e-09 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_57222d-99"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Child Support</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_01c0f0-cb"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Care dependency</span></span></li>

<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_804577-e1"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Disability Grant</span></span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_ce18fe-dc"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Foster Child Grant</span></span></li>

<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_0c6290-03"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Social Relief of Distress</span></span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_708659-99 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_3c2767-e1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><b><strong><b><b><b>What is My SASSA Status Pending?&nbsp;</b></b></b></strong></b></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Unfortunately, for a lot of people, when they check Sassa</span> status online it is only showing as “pending” and they are unable to receive the R350. The official SASSA recently released the below message on 1st June 2026. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Payments for the new cycle of the special COVID-19 SRD grant (from April 2026) will be paid as of mid-June 2026.</span></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">SASSA will continue clearing outstanding payments from the previous cycle as and when the bank details are confirmed. The payments will not be done together but will be done month by month. More than one payment may be made in a month, but no one will receive double payments in amount. SASSA will do these multiple payments in a month until the backlog is finalized, where after monthly payments will resume.</span></p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_298afd-cc alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_654fe4-7e"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><b><strong><b><b><b>How Do I Have My R350 Grant Reconsidered?</b></b></b></strong></b></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">If you see your Covid-19</span> <span style="font-weight: 400;">SRD R350 grant application status as ‘Reapplication Pending’ then you should follow the below steps to dispute your R350 grant status: Go to the SRD portal:</span><a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;"> https://srd.sassa.gov.za</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Click on the ‘Application for Reconsideration’ tab Then select ‘Click here to apply for reconsideration’ Provide your ID number and cellphone number Complete the rest of the steps for reconsideration of your payment.</span></p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_f1c6a0-66 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_a85ea3-3a"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><b><strong><b><b><b>When Does the SASSA R350 Grant End?</b></b></b></strong></b></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">President Cyril Ramaphosa has stated that the Covid-19 R350 government grant and payment of grants will be extended for the next 12 months till March 2026. This was announced during the State of the Nation Address (SONA) in Cape Town on February 10. It is hoped the Relief of Distress Grant will continue to help those people that need it most in South Africa. The grant should be seen as a temporary grant and an opportunity to help those find new career options.</span></p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_fad40a-7b alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_9aa174-5e"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><b><strong><b><b><b>Access Via the SRD SASSA Gov Login</b></b></b></strong></b></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Grant applicants can also check the current SRD grant application status on the official SASSA website here: srd.sassa.gov.za Navigate to the SRD grant application status on the official SASSA website using the online dashboard link here:</span><a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/status" target="_blank" rel="noopener"> <span style="font-weight: 400;">https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/status</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Enter your South African ID number of Applicant Enter the phone number you used to submit the application</span>.</p>

<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_0785c5-92"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Above the age of 18 and below the age of 60</span></span></li>

</ul></div>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_c89788-81"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><b><strong><b><b><b>Why it is Important to Re-apply?&nbsp;</b></b></b></strong></b></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_5a16da-f1 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_1950bd-68"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">People circumstances may have changed over time</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_4d7a8e-dc"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">In order to confirm clients’ personal details, assess their income and financial status</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_e2f1f5-53"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Applicants need to accept the declaration and consent, which has been strengthened to comply with the Protection of Personal Information Act (POPIA) which came into effect on 21 July </span>2026.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_283f0f-79"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">In order to access or to have the application reconsidered for the Social Relief of Distress Grant, an applicant must grant consent for SASSA to verify his or her identity, residency, income, or social security benefits with any other institution deemed necessary by SASSA.</span></span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_3b99b4-36 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_1cc773-19"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><b><strong><b><b><b>SRD R350 Application Status Expected Results</b></b></b></strong></b></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>SRD status checks will return one of the following results. Below I will explain each result and the steps to follow:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items5674_3bb654-ef kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_7efe6c-c1"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-ic_document kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 8 8"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 0v8h7v-4h-4v-4h-3zm4 0v3h3l-3-3zm-3 2h1v1h-1v-1zm0 2h1v1h-1v-1zm0 2h4v1h-4v-1z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Application Complete: </strong>You have completed the application or reapplication process for the SRD R350 grant. Each month, it will be verified before approval. It does not guarantee that you will receive grant payments, but it shows you are on your way to doing so.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_ebbf10-1c"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Application Approved Status: </strong>Your SASSA grant application has been approved when you see &#8220;Approved Status.&#8221;. Once the grant is approved, you&#8217;ll receive the funds. The approval will be notified to you via SMS, email, or letter. After that, you can choose how you want to receive the money: through your bank account, Post Office account, or cash card.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_81b974-89"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_alertCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><line x1="12" y1="8" x2="12" y2="12"/><line x1="12" y1="16" x2="12" y2="16"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Declined Application Status:</strong> When your SASSA status is Declined, it means you did not meet the eligibility criteria and SASSA has rejected your application. SASSA will also provide you with the reason for rejection.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_fce583-41"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-ic_redo kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 8 8"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M3.5 0c-1.93 0-3.5 1.57-3.5 3.5 0-1.38 1.12-2.5 2.5-2.5s2.5 1.12 2.5 2.5v.5h-1l2 2 2-2h-1v-.5c0-1.93-1.57-3.5-3.5-3.5z" transform="translate(0 1)"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Application Status Pending:</strong> SASSA status pending means SASSA has received your application but needs more time to review it and verify your details before approving it. Upon completion of verifications, your grant status will be updated and you will be notified.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-5674_1a2031-21"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_id-card kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 576 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M528 32H48C21.5 32 0 53.5 0 80v16h576V80c0-26.5-21.5-48-48-48zM0 432c0 26.5 21.5 48 48 48h480c26.5 0 48-21.5 48-48V128H0v304zm352-232c0-4.4 3.6-8 8-8h144c4.4 0 8 3.6 8 8v16c0 4.4-3.6 8-8 8H360c-4.4 0-8-3.6-8-8v-16zm0 64c0-4.4 3.6-8 8-8h144c4.4 0 8 3.6 8 8v16c0 4.4-3.6 8-8 8H360c-4.4 0-8-3.6-8-8v-16zm0 64c0-4.4 3.6-8 8-8h144c4.4 0 8 3.6 8 8v16c0 4.4-3.6 8-8 8H360c-4.4 0-8-3.6-8-8v-16zM176 192c35.3 0 64 28.7 64 64s-28.7 64-64 64-64-28.7-64-64 28.7-64 64-64zM67.1 396.2C75.5 370.5 99.6 352 128 352h8.2c12.3 5.1 25.7 8 39.8 8s27.6-2.9 39.8-8h8.2c28.4 0 52.5 18.5 60.9 44.2 3.2 9.9-5.2 19.8-15.6 19.8H82.7c-10.4 0-18.8-10-15.6-19.8z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Identity Verification Failed:</strong> You were unable to verify your identity due to a problem. <div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_08d570-9a"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><b><strong><b><b><b>FAQs About SASSA Status Check</b></b></b></strong></b></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-accordion alignnone"><div class="kt-accordion-wrap kt-accordion-id5674_559ae9-16 kt-accordion-has-37-panes kt-active-pane-0 kt-accordion-block kt-pane-header-alignment-left kt-accodion-icon-style-basic kt-accodion-icon-side-right" style="max-width:none"><div class="kt-accordion-inner-wrap" data-allow-multiple-open="false" data-start-open="0">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-1 kt-pane5674_b647b8-a1"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How Do I Check The Status Of My SRD R350?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Application status checks may fail if the user-provided information does not match the department’s database.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-2 kt-pane5674_a4ba56-48"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How Do I Check The Status Of My SASSA R350 Payment Date 2026?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>For the most up-to-date information about your SASSA R350 payment in 2025, you can contact SASSA directly or visit their official website.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-3 kt-pane5674_2c9d27-d7"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How Do You Check If Your SASSA is in?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>To check if your SASSA payment is in, you can follow these steps:</p>



<p><strong>Visit The Official SASSA Website.</strong></p>



<p></p>



<ol class="wp-block-list">
<li>Look for the “Check Payment Status” or “Payment Enquiry” section.</li>



<li>Enter your personal details, such as your ID number and SASSA reference number.</li>



<li>Submit the information and wait for the system to retrieve your payment status.</li>



<li>Review the displayed information to see if your SASSA payment has been processed and if it is available for collection.</li>
</ol>



<p>Alternatively, you can contact the SASSA helpline or visit your nearest SASSA office for assistance in checking your payment status.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-4 kt-pane5674_b0310a-0d"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What if Sassa status check failed?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>An application status check may fail if the user-provided details don’t match the department of home affairs database.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-6 kt-pane5674_279d1b-87"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What does the means test mean on Sassa’s status?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>In a mean test, the applicant’s data is verified, and he/she is determined to be eligible for the grant or not.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-7 kt-pane5674_84d74b-8c"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How do I check my Sassa status online for free?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>The website sassa-status-check.co.za allows you to check the status of your application at any time.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-8 kt-pane5674_310fe8-45"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>When is Sassa Sassa’s status updated?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Every time Sassa takes a mean test, her status is updated. In the means test, your application confirms whether you are still eligible for the grant. Depending on your current financial situation, the status may change or remain the same.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-9 kt-pane5674_1e8290-81"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>Why can’t I check my Sassa SRD r350 status?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>When you check your Sassa status, you receive the message identification verification fails, which means that the details you enter do not match Department of Home Affairs data. To check your status, you must enter the correct details.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-10 kt-pane5674_2b0edd-d8"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What does not select mean on Sassa status?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>If you do not see your&nbsp;Sassa status&nbsp;selected, that means Sassa has not approved your application. Therefore, you need to reapply for a grant. The decision can also be appealed or a reconsideration request can be made.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-11 kt-pane5674_babd3c-bd"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What does the post office not selected mean by Sassa’s status?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Sassa grants do not require specific post office locations. “Post office not selected” means you can collect your grant from any SAPO branch according to your preferences.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-12 kt-pane5674_3e7343-75"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How to Sassa status check reconsideration application?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p><strong>&nbsp;</strong>Imagine you have been declined for a Sassa grant. Once you confirm your reapplication, you can submit the application for reconsideration. You can view the status of your reconsideration application through the Sassa reconsideration portal:<a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/reconsideration" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">&nbsp;https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/reconsideration</a>. To submit the application, you only need your South African ID number and phone number. Next, you need to navigate to “send pin.”</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-13 kt-pane5674_e70c16-cf"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>Why haven’t I received my Sassa r350?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>There have been numerous instances in which Sassa has been unable to pay applicants due to incorrect information. In some cases, applicants provide incorrect contact information or bank details unintentionally, for example. It is common for applicants to keep updating their bank details, which can delay their grant payments.” Sassa also advised beneficiaries to choose bank details over cardless payment options at ATMs if they want speedier payments.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-14 kt-pane5674_bc4d58-93"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>Why is my Sassa r350 status still pending?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>The Sassa r350 status pending means that your application still needs to be verified and screened, and it has not yet been approved. When Sassa approves your application, you’ll receive an SMS from the Sassa official requesting your bank details.&nbsp;</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-15 kt-pane5674_9634f8-87"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How do I check my Sassa SRD status check balance?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>In order to dial this number, dial *120*69277# on your phone. You will receive an SMS notification about your balance status if you follow the instructions on the phone call.&nbsp;<strong>SASSA SRD Status check and balance Online</strong></p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-16 kt-pane5674_50fe1e-29"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How do I check my Sassa status on Govchat?&nbsp;</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>The go chat app allows you to check your status:</p>



<p></p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
