<li>The following email addresses are available:&nbsp;<a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="7605041236051705051758111900580c17">[email&#160;protected]</a></li>



<li>The website address is:<a href="http://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">&nbsp;http://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/</a>.</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-17 kt-pane5674_d3a339-82"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How do I check my Sassa payment status?&nbsp;</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>The south African Sassa agency announces the R350 Social Relief Grant payment status schedule every month. The organization distributes grants and provides people with special Covid 19 benefits.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-18 kt-pane5674_05daa7-63"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How long does Sassa take to get paid?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>The application process may take up to three months. Beneficiaries will receive their payments once the</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-19 kt-pane5674_e86640-9b"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>After Sassa’s status approval, how long does it take to pay?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>As soon as the grant application has been approved, Sassa will pay the beneficiaries. Upon receiving their grant payment, the beneficiaries can collect their money through a bank, cash send, or a retailer, such as Checker, Usave, Shoprite, Pick’n Pay, Boxer, etc. Through the online portal, beneficiaries can check the status of their grants at any time:<a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/status" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">&nbsp;https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/status</a>.&nbsp;</p>



<p>In order to retail for grant money, the beneficiaries must provide their ID document and a cell phone with the number registered at the time of application. As a quick and safe method of transferring money, Sassa preferred the bank option. Those who collect their grants through the post office should withdraw their funds through retail outlets, according to the Sassa.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-20 kt-pane5674_20bd94-42"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How can I check my SASSA details?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>The Sassa online portal service allows beneficiaries to check their details anytime.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-21 kt-pane5674_8ccfc5-35"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What does grant application status active mean?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>As soon as you submit your application, your Sassa grant status shows active, which means that Sassa has successfully received your application. Your fund approval decision will be announced once it has been announced.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-22 kt-pane5674_e7fb36-11"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What does it mean when SASSA Status says the application is complete?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>It states application complete, which means that your reapplication process was successful, and your application will go through the verification process each month to confirm that you are eligible to receive the grant. Every month, you should check your Sassa status on the Sassa SRD website.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-23 kt-pane5674_fef653-e2"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How long is SRD reconsideration pending status?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Once you file an appeal or reconsider your application, the Sassa will inform you of the outcome within 60 to 90 days.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-24 kt-pane5674_f60909-76"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>Sassa status approved but did not receive SMS from SASSA?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>In that case, you must check whether your personal information such as your phone number is correct or not. Your Sassa status is approved, but you did not receive an SMS from Sassa. For immediate assistance, you can also contact the nearest Sassa office or call the Sassa helpline.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-25 kt-pane5674_e9a7cd-e2"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What does Sassa’s status reapplication pending means?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>The Sassa agency did not receive any applications or reapplications. In this case, you will have to wait until Sassa receives your application or resubmit it properly.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-26 kt-pane5674_4b2d1c-bb"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What does Sassa’s application status approval mean?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Sassa’s application has been approved for the period mentioned there. It is now the applicant’s responsibility to check the status of the pay date. In the absence of a payment date, the payment has not yet been processed.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-27 kt-pane5674_f0f1bf-14"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What does Sassa’s application status bank detail pending means?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>The Sassa application bank details pending means Sassa did not receive any kind of payment method or information from you.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-28 kt-pane5674_22ff77-f1"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What does Sassa’s status canceled means?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>According to the mean test, your grant has been canceled because you may have other grants, funds, income resources, or employment.</p>



<p>By providing your ID number and the mobile number associated with your grant, you can also ask them to check Sassa’s online application status.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-29 kt-pane5674_b83d77-64"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How To Reconfirm Your Existing Application through status check?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Reconfirming your existing application through Sassa status is as simple as visiting the Sassa website. Visit<a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">&nbsp;https://srd.sassa.gov.za</a>. Look for the tab that says “Reconfirm your grant application.” Click the yellow bar button and enter the information according to the instructions.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-30 kt-pane5674_2550c5-52"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What is the check status of the Sassa r350 appeal?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>By calling the Sassa toll-free number 0800601011 you can check the status of your Sassa r350 appeal. When speaking with Sassa officials, you need to have your ID number and phone number on hand.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-31 kt-pane5674_ab434b-d2"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How to check Sassa’s SRD balance status?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Sassa SRD balance status can be checked through your bank account, but there is no specific method available for checking it. Directly contacting the post office to check their Sassa payment status is an option for Sassa beneficiaries who receive their payments through cash send or by the post office. Your ID and phone number are all you need. There is no charge for this service.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-32 kt-pane5674_4567a1-2b"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What is Sassa’s status pin?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p><strong>&nbsp;</strong>In order to apply for the Sassa R350 grant, beneficiaries must receive a one-time OTP code called the Sassa status pin. You will receive the pin on the phone number you provided.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-33 kt-pane5674_6d27ef-ff"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What does declined to mean on Sassa status check?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>If you receive a declined status on&nbsp;Sassa status check, it means that the information you submitted during application submission does not match the information in the home affairs department’s database, such as your surname, name, ID number, etc.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-34 kt-pane5674_2f4609-a7"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What does approved mean by Sassa’s status check?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>If your grant is approved, you will receive R350 in your bank account.</p>



<p>If Your grant has been declined, which means there is an issue with your credentials or documentation, and you have 30 days to file an appeal.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-35 kt-pane5674_8f5c10-b7"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What does Sassa status check pending means?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>If your status is pending, it means your allowed date has not been met or there has been a delay in the transaction.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-37 kt-pane5674_5dd672-8f"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>If you have other queries related to Sassa’s online application status?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>The Toll-Free number 0800601011 can be used to inquire about Sassa’s unemployment grant.</p>



<p>Sassa has approved your grant application but has not announced a payment date yet, so your payment has not been processed. As soon as it is processed, Sassa will send you an SMS regarding the collection of your grant payment to the phone number you provided during the application process. In order for your grant application to be approved, your phone number must be registered in your name.</p>
</div></div></div>
</div></div></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id5674_2aa758-11 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column5674_34ab8a-4c"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><b><strong><b><b><b>Conclusion</b></b></b></strong></b></b></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>We Hope all confusion is clear about the SASSA Status Check online. If you have any problem with SASSA please contact with contact us page. Thank You.</p>
